return {}; } } function notesPlainText_(raw) { if (raw == null || raw === "") return ""; return String(raw) .replace(//gi, "\n") .replace(/<[^>]+>/g, "") .replace(/ /g, " ") .trim(); } function toothKeyToShortLabel_(key) { const m = String(key || "").match(/^(upper|lower)_(L|R)(\d+)$/); if (!m) return String(key || ""); const jaw = m[1] === "upper" ? "上" : "下"; const side = m[2] === "L" ? "右" : "左"; return jaw + side + m[3]; } function extractFkyokuTeethFromTeethData_(teethData) { const teeth = []; const labels = []; if (!teethData || typeof teethData !== "object") return { teeth, labels }; Object.keys(teethData).forEach(k => { if (!/^(upper|lower)_(L|R)\d+$/.test(k)) return; const cond = String(teethData[k] || ""); if (!cond) return; const parts = parseTeethCondParts(cond); if (parts.known.includes("F局") || cond.indexOf("F局") !== -1) { teeth.push(k); labels.push(toothKeyToShortLabel_(k)); } }); return { teeth, labels }; } function parseExamValueFromNotes_(notes, code) { const s = notesPlainText_(notes); if (!s) return null; if (code === PERIODIC_EXAM_TONGUE_) { const m = s.match(/舌圧[^\d]*(\d+\.?\d*)\s*(?:kPa|kpa|キロパスカル)?/i); if (m) return { value: m[1], unit: "kPa" }; } if (code === PERIODIC_EXAM_MOISTURE_) { const m = s.match(/(?:湿潤|粘膜)[^\d]*(\d+\.?\d*)\s*点/) || s.match(/(\d+\.?\d*)\s*点[^\d]*(?:湿潤|粘膜)/); if (m) return { value: m[1], unit: "点" }; } return null; } function findNearestTeethSnapshot_(teethHistory, visitYmd) { if (!teethHistory || !teethHistory.length || !visitYmd) return null; const target = formatDateInputVal(visitYmd) || String(visitYmd).slice(0, 10); let bestOnOrBefore = null; teethHistory.forEach(snap => { const d = formatDateInputVal(snap.date) || String(snap.date || "").slice(0, 10); if (!d || d > target) return; if (!bestOnOrBefore || d > bestOnOrBefore.date) bestOnOrBefore = { date: d, json: snap.json }; }); if (bestOnOrBefore) return bestOnOrBefore; let bestAny = null; let bestDiff = Infinity; const tMs = parseYmdNoon_(target); teethHistory.forEach(snap => { const d = formatDateInputVal(snap.date) || String(snap.date || "").slice(0, 10); const dMs = parseYmdNoon_(d); if (!dMs || isNaN(dMs.getTime())) return; const diff = Math.abs(dMs.getTime() - (tMs && !isNaN(tMs.getTime()) ? tMs.getTime() : 0)); if (diff < bestDiff) { bestDiff = diff; bestAny = { date: d, json: snap.json }; } }); return bestAny; } function buildPatientExamHistory_(records, teethHistory) { const rows = []; (records || []).forEach(rec => { const ymd = formatDateInputVal(rec.visit_date) || ""; if (!ymd) return; const examData = parseExamDataField_(rec.exam_data); PERIODIC_EXAM_TYPES_.forEach(t => { if (!recordHasTreatment_(rec, t.code)) return; let value = ""; let unit = t.unit; let detail = ""; const saved = examData[t.code]; if (saved && typeof saved === "object") { if (t.code === PERIODIC_EXAM_FKYOKU_) { const lbs = saved.labels && saved.labels.length ? String(rec.id) : "", date: ymd, dateDisp: formatVisitDateDisp(rec.visit_date), exam: t.label, examCode: t.code, value, unit, detail }); }); }); rows.sort((a, b) => b.date.localeCompare(a.date) || a.exam.localeCompare(b.exam, "ja")); return rows; } function renderExamInputs_() { const wrap = document.getElementById("examInputsWrap"); const rowT = document.getElementById("examInputTongue"); const rowM = document.getElementById("examInputMoisture"); const rowF = document.getElementById("examInputFkyoku"); if (!wrap) return; const hasT = selectedTreatments.has(PERIODIC_EXAM_TONGUE_); const hasM = selectedTreatments.has(PERIODIC_EXAM_MOISTURE_); const hasF = selectedTreatments.has(PERIODIC_EXAM_FKYOKU_); const any = hasT || hasM || hasF; wrap.style.display = any ? } catch (_) { const y = next.getFullYear(); const m = String(next.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, "0"); return `${y}-${m}-01`; } } function recordTreatmentList_(rec) { return String(rec.treatments || "") .split(/[、,]/) .map(s => s.trim()) .filter(Boolean); } /** 診療記録から前回実施日（いちばん新しい visit_date） */ function getLastRestrictedTreatmentDate_(pid, treatmentCode, opts) { opts = opts || {}; let latest = ""; (localRecords || []).forEach(r => { if (String(r.patient_id) !== String(pid)) return; if (typeof v === "object" && v !== null && typeof v.getTime === "function" && !isNaN(v.getTime())) { try { return new Intl.DateTimeFormat("sv-SE", { timeZone: "Asia/Tokyo" }).format(v).slice(0, 10); } catch (_) {} } let s = typeof v === "string" ? v : String(v); if (/^\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}T/.test(s) || /^\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}[-+]\d{2}:/.test(s)) { const d = new Date(s); if (!isNaN(d.getTime())) { try { return new Intl.DateTimeFormat("sv-SE", { timeZone: "Asia/Tokyo" }).format(d).slice(0, 10); } catch (_) {} } } if (s.indexOf("T") !== -1) s = s.split("T")[0]; let m = s.match(/^(\d{4})[-/.／](\d{1,2})[-/.／](\d{1,2})/); if (m) { const mo = String(Math.min(12, Math.max(1, parseInt(m[2], 10)))).padStart(2, "0"); const d = String(Math.min(31, Math.max(1, parseInt(m[3], 10)))).padStart(2, "0"); return `${m[1]}-${mo}-${d}`; } m = s.match(/^(\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2})/); return m ? m[1] : ""; } /** input[type=time] 用 HH:mm */ function formatTimeForInput_(v) { if (v == null || v === "") return ""; const s0 = String(v).trim(); const m = s0.match(/^(\d{1,2}):(\d{2})/); if (m) { const h = Math.min(23, Math.max(0, parseInt(m[1], 10))); const mi = Math.min(59, Math.max(0, parseInt(m[2], 10))); return `${String(h).padStart(2, "0")}:${String(mi).padStart(2, "0")}`; } const d = new Date(s0); if (!isNaN(d.getTime())) { return `${String(d.getHours()).padStart(2, "0")}:${String(d.getMinutes()).padStart(2, "0")}`; } return ""; } /** 診療時間：分を加算（同日にクランプ。24:00 超は 23:59） */ function addMinutesClampedSameDay_(h, m, deltaMin) { let t = Math.round(h) * 60 + Math.round(m) + deltaMin; } /** 終了：数字 → hidden（開始の自動入力とは独立） */ function commitVisitTimeEnd_() { const hEl = document.getElementById("visitTimeEndH"); const mEl = document.getElementById("visitTimeEndM"); const hid = document.getElementById("visitTimeEnd"); `; } /** * セル表示用：処置後（_red）と初期所見＋コメントを分離（別行表示用）。 * 赤はマスタ記号のうち _red に列挙されたものだけ。自由文・その他記号は黒行。 */ /** セル内の表示行数（記号トークン数＋EXT）から min-height を決める */ function estimateTeethCellLineCount_(blackText, redText, hasExt) { var n = 0; if (hasExt) n += 1; if (redText) { n += String(redText).split(/[+＋]/).map(function (s) { return s.trim(); }).filter(Boolean).length; } if (blackText) { n += String(blackText).split(/[+＋]/).map(function (s) { return s.trim(); }).filter(Boolean).length; } return n; } function teethCellMinHeightPx_(lineCount) { if (lineCount <= 1) return 52; return 34 + lineCount * 15; } function splitTeethDisplayLines_(cond, redStr) { const { known, unknown } = parseTeethCondParts(cond || ""); const filt = known.filter(k => k !== "EXT" && k !== "Br"); const reds = new Set((redStr || "").split(/[+＋]/).map(s => s.trim()).filter(Boolean)); const redToks = filt.filter(k => reds.has(k)); const blackToks = filt.filter(k => !reds.has(k)); const blackText = mergeTeethParts(blackToks, unknown); const redText = mergeTeethParts(redToks, []); return { blackText, redText }; } /** 歯式セル内の短文表示から EXT・Br を除く（抜歯・ブリッジは別表示） */ function condSymbolsForCellBody(cond) { const { known, unknown } = parseTeethCondParts(cond || ""); const filt = known.filter(k => k !== "EXT" && k !== "Br"); return mergeTeethParts(filt, unknown); } function toothHasBr(cond) { return parseTeethCondParts(cond || "").known.includes("Br"); } function buildToothKeys(jaw, nums) { const mid = nums.length / 2; return nums.map((n, i) => `${jaw}_${i < mid ? "L" : "R"}${n}`); } /** Br 支台と欠損（ポンティック）で挟まれた区間をブリッジとして結ぶ */ function isPonticTooth(key, data) { return !!data[key + "_miss"]; } function isSolidToothKey(key, data) { return !isPonticTooth(key, data); } /** 隣の残存歯に所見または Br がある（健全空欄とはブリッジで結ばない） */ function hasAbutmentLikeContent(key, data) { if (isPonticTooth(key, data)) return false; const c = (data[key] || "").trim(); if (c) return true; return false; } /** * Br は片側の支台にだけ付ければよい。 * ・その Br から左右に欠損だけを走査し、最初に当たる残存歯までをブリッジとして結ぶ（両側に Br 不要）。 * ・欠損ゼロの隣接は、隣歯に所見または Br があるときだけ短い線（カンチレバ等）を描く。 * ・延長 Br は両支台に Br を付けたあと、片側を欠損（ポンティック）にすると一望できる。 */ function findBridgeSpans(keys, data) { const seen = new Set(); const out = []; const add = (a, b) => { if (a === b) return; if (a > b) [a, b] = [b, a]; const k = `${a}-${b}`; if (seen.has(k)) return; seen.add(k); out.push([a, b]); }; for (let i = 0; i < keys.length; i++) { if (!toothHasBr(data[keys[i]] || "")) continue; let r = i + 1; let missR = 0; while (r < keys.length && isPonticTooth(keys[r], data)) { missR++; r++; } if (missR > 0 && r < keys.length && isSolidToothKey(keys[r], data)) add(i, r); let l = i - 1; let missL = 0; while (l >= 0 && isPonticTooth(keys[l], data)) { missL++; l--; } if (missL > 0 && l >= 0 && isSolidToothKey(keys[l], data)) add(l, i); if (i + 1 < keys.length && isSolidToothKey(keys[i + 1], data)) { if (hasAbutmentLikeContent(keys[i + 1], data) || toothHasBr(data[keys[i + 1]] || "")) add(i, i + 1); } if (i - 1 >= 0 && isSolidToothKey(keys[i - 1], data)) { if (hasAbutmentLikeContent(keys[i - 1], data) || toothHasBr(data[keys[i - 1]] || "")) add(i - 1, i); } } return out; } function bracketEndpointLabel(cond) { const { known, unknown } = parseTeethCondParts(cond || ""); const parts = known.filter(x => x !== "Br" && x !== "EXT"); if (parts.length) return parts[0]; if (unknown.length) return unknown[0].slice(0, 10); return ""; } /** Br 非表示にした隣接歯列インデックスの辺（例: "11-12" = keys[11] と keys[12] の間） */ function bridgeHiddenEdgeKey_(i, j) { const a = Math.min(i, j); const b = Math.max(i, j); return a + "-" + b; } function bridgeHiddenSet_(data, jaw) { const k = jaw === "upper" ? "bridge_hide_upper" : "bridge_hide_lower"; return new Set(String(data[k] || "").split(/[,+]/).map(s => s.trim()).filter(Boolean)); } function setBridgeHiddenSet_(data, jaw, set) { const k = jaw === "upper" ? "bridge_hide_upper" : "bridge_hide_lower"; const arr = [...set].sort(); if (!arr.length) delete data[k]; else data[k] = arr.join(","); } /** 横線の実効端 [lo,hi]（findBridgeSpans の端点そのまま） */ function bridgeEffectiveEndpoints_(_keys, _data, _jaw, ia, ib) { return [Math.min(ia, ib), Math.max(ia, ib)]; } /** ブリッジに含まれない辺キーは削除（歯式変更後のゴミ防止） */ function pruneBridgeHideEdges_(keys, data, jaw) { const k = jaw === "upper" ? "bridge_hide_upper" : "bridge_hide_lower"; if (!data[k]) return; const spans = findBridgeSpans(keys, data); const valid = new Set(); spans.forEach(function (span) { const eff = bridgeEffectiveEndpoints_(keys, data, jaw, span[0], span[1]); const lo = eff[0]; const hi = eff[1]; for (let j = lo; j < hi; j++) valid.add(bridgeHiddenEdgeKey_(j, j + 1)); }); const cur = bridgeHiddenSet_(data, jaw); const next = new Set(); cur.forEach(function (e) { if (valid.has(e)) next.add(e); }); setBridgeHiddenSet_(data, jaw, next); } /** 単位辺 [j,j+1] の配列を連結ラン [start,end]（インデックス）にまとめる */ function mergeBridgeUnitEdges_(units) { const u = units.slice().sort(function (a, b) { return a[0] - b[0]; }); const runs = []; let rs = -1; let re = -1; u.forEach(function (pair) { const a = pair[0]; const b = pair[1]; if (rs < 0) { rs = a; re = b; return; } if (a === re) re = b; else { runs.push([rs, re]); rs = a; re = b; } }); if (rs >= 0) runs.push([rs, re]); return runs; } const TEETH_CHART_CELL = 44; const TEETH_CHART_GAP = 3; function bridgeOverlayHtml(keys, data, jaw) { const CELL = TEETH_CHART_CELL; const GAP = TEETH_CHART_GAP; const step = CELL + GAP; const n = keys.length; const totalW = n * CELL + (n - 1) * GAP; const spans = findBridgeSpans(keys, data); if (!spans.length) return ""; const hide = bridgeHiddenSet_(data, jaw); const cx = i => i * step + CELL / 2; const stroke = "#334155"; const sw = 2; const hitSw = 14; const H = 28; let body = ""; const yBar = jaw === "upper" ? 15 : H - 4; const yLeg = jaw === "upper" ? 24 : 5; const textY = jaw === "upper" ? 11 : H - 1; spans.forEach(function (span) { let ia = span[0]; let ib = span[1]; if (ia > ib) { const t = ia; ia = ib; ib = t; } const eff = bridgeEffectiveEndpoints_(keys, data, jaw, ia, ib); const effLo = eff[0]; const effHi = eff[1]; if (effLo >= effHi) return; const visibleUnits = []; const hiddenUnits = []; for (let j = effLo; j < effHi; j++) { const ek = bridgeHiddenEdgeKey_(j, j + 1); if (hide.has(ek)) hiddenUnits.push([j, j + 1]); else visibleUnits.push([j, j + 1]); } if (!visibleUnits.length && !hiddenUnits.length) return; visibleUnits.forEach(function (pair) { const j = pair[0]; const jp = pair[1]; const x1 = cx(j); const x2 = cx(jp); const ek = bridgeHiddenEdgeKey_(j, jp); body += ``; body += ``; body += ``; body += ``; }); hiddenUnits.forEach(function (pair) { const j = pair[0]; const jp = pair[1]; const x1 = cx(j); const x2 = cx(jp); const ek = bridgeHiddenEdgeKey_(j, jp); body += ``; }); if (!visibleUnits.length) return; if (visibleUnits.length) { const runs = mergeBridgeUnitEdges_(visibleUnits); runs.forEach(function (run) { const rs = run[0]; const re = run[1]; const labL = escHtml(bracketEndpointLabel(data[keys[rs]] || "")); const labR = escHtml(bracketEndpointLabel(data[keys[re]] || "")); if (labL) body += `${labL}`; if (labR && re !== rs) body += `${labR}`; }); } const legAt = new Set(); visibleUnits.forEach(function (pair) { legAt.add(pair[0]); legAt.add(pair[1]); }); for (let bi = effLo; bi <= effHi; bi++) { if (toothHasBr(data[keys[bi]] || "") && !isPonticTooth(keys[bi], data)) legAt.add(bi); } legAt.forEach(function (j) { if (isPonticTooth(keys[j], data)) return; body += ``; }); }); return `

dementiaLevel:"" }; /** 疾患・服薬の1件を { name, onsetYear, onsetMonth, displayName? } に正規化（旧データの文字列も受ける） */ function normalizeMedEntry_(e) { if (e == null) return null; if (typeof e === "string") { const n = e.trim(); return n ? { name: n, onsetYear: "", onsetMonth: "" } : null; } if (typeof e === "object" && e.name) { const name = String(e.name).trim(); const out = { name, onsetYear: e.onsetYear != null ? String(e.displayName).trim() : ""; if (dn && dn !== name) out.displayName = dn; return out; } return null; } function medEntryName_(e) { if (typeof e === "string") return String(e).trim(); if (e && typeof e === "object" && e.name) return String(e.name).trim(); return ""; } /** 発症年：H30 / R5 / 平成30 / 2020 などを保存用に正規化 */ function normalizeOnsetYearInput_(raw) { var s = String(raw == null ? "" : raw).trim(); if (!s) return ""; var m = s.match(/^([RHSrhs])[.\s]*(\d{1,2})$/); if (m) return m[1].toUpperCase() + m[2]; m = s.match(/^(令和|平成|昭和)[.\s]*(\d{1,2})$/); if (m) { var map = { "令和": "R", "平成": "H", "昭和": "S" }; return map[m[1]] + m[2]; } if (/^\d{4}$/.test(s)) return s; return s; } function findMedEntryIndex_(type, name) { const arr = type === "diseases" ? patientMedical.conditions : patientMedical.medications; const key = String(name || "").trim(); if (!key) return -1; var ix = arr.findIndex(function (e) { return medEntryName_(e) === key; }); if (ix >= 0) return ix; if (type === "meds") ix = arr.findIndex(function (e) { return medStoredMatchesToggleItem_(e, key); }); if (ix >= 0) return ix; if (type === "diseases") ix = arr.findIndex(function (e) { return diseasePatientMatchesToggleLabel_(e, key); }); return ix; } /** 画面上の発症入力を patientMedical に反映（保存ボタン直前用） */ function flushMedOnsetFromDom_() { ["diseases", "meds"].forEach(function (type) { const el = document.getElementById("sel-" + type); if (!el) return; el.querySelectorAll("[data-med-onset-year]").forEach(function (inp) { const name = inp.getAttribute("data-med-name"); if (name) updateMedOnset(type, name, "year", inp.value, { skipSave: true }); }); el.querySelectorAll("[data-med-onset-month]").forEach(function (inp) { const name = inp.getAttribute("data-med-name"); if (name) updateMedOnset(type, name, "month", inp.value, { skipSave: true }); }); }); } /** 疾患・服薬共通：画面上の表示名（マスタ連動・リスク判定は name のまま） */ function medEntryDisplay_(e) { if (typeof e === "string") return String(e).trim(); if (e && typeof e === "object" && e.name) { const name = String(e.name).trim(); const dn = e.displayName != null ? "疾患の表示名を入力してください（一覧の選択・リスクは元の病名に基づきます）" : "服薬の表示名を入力してください（一覧の選択・リスクは元の薬名に基づきます）"; const next = prompt(hint, curShow); if (next === null) return; const t = String(next).trim(); if (!t || t === cur.name) delete cur.displayName; else cur.displayName = t; arr[ix] = normalizeMedEntry_(cur); renderSelectedTags(type); renderRiskAlerts(); saveMedicalInfo(); } /** 服薬マスタ1行の表示・保存キー（商品名があるときは「一般名（商品名）」） */ function medMasterEntryKey_(m) { if (!m || !m.name) return ""; const nm = String(m.name).trim(); const br = m.brand != null ? String(m.brand).trim() : ""; return br ? `${nm}（${br}）` : nm; } /** 手入力「一般名（商品名）」を分解（カスタムマスタ登録用） */ function parseManualMedLabel_(val) { const s = String(val || "").trim(); const hit = /^(.+?)（([^）]+)）\s*$/.exec(s); if (hit) return { name: hit[1].trim(), brand: hit[2].trim() }; return { name: s, brand: "" }; } /** 患者の服薬エントリがマスタ行と同じ薬か（保存が一般名のみの旧データも一致。マスタ名称変更前の表記も一致） */ function medEntryMatchesMaster_(e, m) { const key = medMasterEntryKey_(m); const n = medEntryName_(e); if (n === key || n === m.name) return true; const parsed = parseManualMedLabel_(key); if (parsed.brand && n === parsed.name) return true; if (m._masterOrigKey) { if (n === m._masterOrigKey) return true; const po = parseManualMedLabel_(m._masterOrigKey); if (po.brand && n === po.name) return true; if (n === po.name) return true; } return false; } /** 一覧クリック時の item（一般名（商品名））と、保存済みエントリが同じ薬か */ function medStoredMatchesToggleItem_(e, toggleItem) { const n = medEntryName_(e); if (n === toggleItem) return true; const parsed = parseManualMedLabel_(toggleItem); if (parsed.brand && n === parsed.name) return true; for (let i = 0; i < medMasterRowEdits.length; i++) { const ed = medMasterRowEdits[i]; const o = parseManualMedLabel_(oldK); if (o.brand && n === o.name) return true; } return false; } function medCategoryForMedicationLabel_(label) { const s = String(label || "").trim(); const parsed = parseManualMedLabel_(s); const baseName = parsed.name || s; const built = MED_MASTER.find(m => medMasterEntryKey_(m) === s || m.name === baseName); if (built && built.cat) return built.cat; const cm = normalizeCustomMedsEntries(customMeds).find(m => medMasterEntryKey_(m) === s || m.name === baseName); if (s === oldK || s === ed.origName) return displayCatForType_("meds", ed.sourceCat); const o = parseManualMedLabel_(oldK); if (o.brand && s === o.name) return displayCatForType_("meds", ed.sourceCat); } return "その他"; } function medCategoryColor_(cat) { const palette = [ "#2563eb", "#0d9488", "#7c3aed", "#ea580c", "#dc2626", "#16a34a", "#0891b2", "#9333ea", "#ca8a04", "#be123c", "#4f46e5", "#64748b" ]; const s = String(cat || "その他"); let h = 0; for (let i = 0; i < s.length; i++) h = (h * 31 + s.charCodeAt(i)) >>> 0; return palette[h % palette.length]; } /** 一般名のみの保存を、マスタ上わかる範囲で「一般名（商品名）」に広げる */ function expandMedEntryWithKnownBrand_(entry) { const e = normalizeMedEntry_(entry); if (!e || !e.name) return e; const n = e.name; if (/（[^）]+）\s*$/.test(n)) return e; const built = MED_MASTER.find(m => m.name === n && m.brand); if (built) return { ...e, name: medMasterEntryKey_(built) }; } function applyExpandedMedicationsIfNeeded_() { const prev = patientMedical.medications || []; const next = prev.map(expandMedEntryWithKnownBrand_); const same = next.length === prev.length && next.every((e, i) => medEntryName_(e) === medEntryName_(prev[i])); if (same) return false; patientMedical.medications = next; return true; } let customDiseases = []; let customMeds = []; let customDiseaseCats = []; let customMedCats = []; /** カテゴリータブの表示順（空ならマスタ由来の既定順） */ let diseaseCategoryOrder = []; /** 組込みマスタ疾患の病名上書き */ let diseaseMasterRowEdits = []; let medFilter = { diseases: "all", meds: "all" }; /** settings 由来のカスタム疾患（{cat,name}[]） */ function normalizeCustomDiseasesEntries(arr) { if (!Array.isArray(arr)) return []; return arr.map(x => { if (typeof x === "string") return { cat: "その他", name: x.trim() }; if (x && typeof x === "object" && x.name) return { cat: String(x.cat || "その他").trim() || "その他", name: String(x.name).trim() }; return null; }).filter(Boolean); } /** settings 由来のカスタム薬（{cat,name,brand}[]） */ function normalizeCustomMedsEntries(arr) { if (!Array.isArray(arr)) return []; return arr.map(x => { if (typeof x === "string") return { cat: "その他", name: x.trim(), brand: "" }; String(x.brand).trim() : "" }; } return null; }).filter(Boolean); } function normalizeMasterCategoryList_(arr) { if (!Array.isArray(arr)) return []; return [...new Set(arr.map(x => String(x || "").trim()).filter(Boolean))]; } function normalizeHiddenMasterEntries_(arr) { if (!Array.isArray(arr)) return []; return arr.map(x => { if (!x || typeof x !== "object") return null; const cat = String(x.cat || "").trim(); const name = String(x.name || "").trim(); return cat && name ? { cat, name } : null; }).filter(Boolean); } function normalizeCategoryRenames_(obj) { if (!obj || typeof obj !== "object" || Array.isArray(obj)) return {}; const out = {}; Object.entries(obj).forEach(([k, v]) => { const oldCat = String(k || "").trim(); const newCat = String(v || "").trim(); if (oldCat && newCat && oldCat !== newCat) out[oldCat] = newCat; }); return out; } function categoryRenamesForType_(type) { return type === "diseases" ? hiddenDiseaseItems : hiddenMedItems; } function displayCatForType_(type, sourceCat) { const renames = categoryRenamesForType_(type); const src = String(sourceCat || "その他").trim() || "その他"; return renames[src] || src; } function isHiddenMasterItem_(type, sourceCat, name) { const cat = String(sourceCat || "").trim(); const nm = String(name || "").trim(); return hiddenItemsForType_(type).some(e => e.cat === cat && e.name === nm); } /** マスタから得られるカテゴリの既定順（保存順が無いときの基準） */ function collectCategoriesDefaultOrder_(type, entries) { const out = []; const seen = new Set(); function add(c) { const v = String(c || "").trim(); if (!v || seen.has(v)) return; seen.add(v); out.push(v); } entries.forEach(e => add(e.cat)); customCategoriesForType_(type).forEach(add); if (!seen.has("その他")) add("その他"); return out; } function normalizeCategoryDisplayOrder_(arr) { if (!Array.isArray(arr)) return []; const out = []; const seen = new Set(); arr.forEach(x => { const v = String(x || "").trim(); if (!v || seen.has(v)) return; seen.add(v); out.push(v); }); return out; } function uniqueDisplayCategories_(type, entries) { const all = collectCategoriesDefaultOrder_(type, entries); const saved = normalizeCategoryDisplayOrder_(type === "diseases" ? diseaseCategoryOrder : medCategoryOrder); if (!saved.length) return all; const set = new Set(all); const out = []; const seen = new Set(); saved.forEach(c => { if (set.has(c) && !seen.has(c)) { out.push(c); seen.add(c); } }); all.forEach(c => { if (!seen.has(c)) { out.push(c); seen.add(c); } }); return out; } function normalizeMedMasterRowEdits_(arr) { if (!Array.isArray(arr)) return []; return arr.map(x => { if (!x || typeof x !== "object") return null; const sourceCat = String(x.sourceCat || "").trim(); const origName = String(x.origName || "").trim(); const name = String(x.name || "").trim(); if (!sourceCat || !origName || !name) return null; return { sourceCat, origName, origBrand: x.origBrand != null ? String(x.origBrand).trim() : "", name, brand: x.brand != null ? String(x.brand).trim() : "" }; }).filter(Boolean); } function normalizeDiseaseMasterRowEdits_(arr) { if (!Array.isArray(arr)) return []; return arr.map(x => { if (!x || typeof x !== "object") return null; const sourceCat = String(x.sourceCat || "").trim(); const origName = String(x.origName || "").trim(); const name = String(x.name || "").trim(); if (!sourceCat || !origName || !name) return null; return { sourceCat, origName, name }; }).filter(Boolean); } function findMedMasterRowEdit_(sourceCat, origName, origBrand) { const br = origBrand != null ? String(origBrand).trim() : ""; return medMasterRowEdits.find(e => e.sourceCat === sourceCat && e.origName === origName && String(e.origBrand || "") === br ); } function findDiseaseMasterRowEdit_(sourceCat, origName) { return diseaseMasterRowEdits.find(e => e.sourceCat === sourceCat && e.origName === origName); } function diseaseEntryMatchesMasterList_(e, listName, sourceCat) { const n = medEntryName_(e); if (n === listName) return true; return diseaseMasterRowEdits.some(ed => ed.sourceCat === sourceCat && ed.name === listName && ed.origName === n ); } function diseasePatientMatchesToggleLabel_(e, toggleLabel) { const n = medEntryName_(e); if (n === toggleLabel) return true; return diseaseMasterRowEdits.some(ed => ed.name === toggleLabel && ed.origName === n); } function persistMasterPrefs_() { return gasCall("saveSettings", JSON.stringify({ custom_disease_categories: JSON.stringify(customDiseaseCats), custom_med_categories: JSON.stringify(customMedCats), hidden_disease_master_items: JSON.stringify(hiddenDiseaseItems), hidden_med_master_items: JSON.stringify(hiddenMedItems), disease_category_renames: JSON.stringify(diseaseCatRenames), med_category_renames: JSON.stringify(medCatRenames), disease_category_order: JSON.stringify(diseaseCategoryOrder), med_category_order: JSON.stringify(medCategoryOrder), med_master_row_edits: JSON.stringify(medMasterRowEdits), disease_master_row_edits: JSON.stringify(diseaseMasterRowEdits), custom_diseases: JSON.stringify(customDiseases), custom_medications: JSON.stringify(customMeds) })); } function diseaseMasterEntries_() { const entries = []; Object.entries(DISEASE_MASTER).forEach(([sourceCat, arr]) => { arr.forEach(origName => { if (!isHiddenMasterItem_("diseases", sourceCat, origName)) { const ed = findDiseaseMasterRowEdit_(sourceCat, origName); const dispName = ed ? ed.name : origName; entries.push({ sourceCat, cat: displayCatForType_("diseases", sourceCat), name: dispName, _custom: false, _delHideName: origName, _masterOrigName: ed ? origName : undefined }); } }); }); normalizeCustomDiseasesEntries(customDiseases).forEach(e => { if (!isHiddenMasterItem_("diseases", e.cat, e.name)) { entries.push({ sourceCat: e.cat, cat: displayCatForType_("diseases", e.cat), name: e.name, _custom: true, _delHideName: e.name }); } }); return entries; } function medMasterEntries_() { const entries = []; MED_MASTER.forEach(origM => { if (!isHiddenMasterItem_("meds", origM.cat, origM.name)) { const ed = findMedMasterRowEdit_(origM.cat, origM.name, origM.brand); const name = ed ? ed.name : origM.name; const brand = ed ? String(ed.brand || "").trim() : (origM.brand != null ? String(origM.brand).trim() : ""); entries.push({ cat: displayCatForType_("meds", origM.cat), sourceCat: origM.cat, name, brand, _custom: false, _delHideName: origM.name, _origMedBrand: origM.brand != null ? String(origM.brand).trim() : "", _masterOrigKey: ed ? medMasterEntryKey_(origM) : undefined }); } }); normalizeCustomMedsEntries(customMeds).forEach(m => { if (!isHiddenMasterItem_("meds", m.cat, m.name)) { entries.push({ cat: displayCatForType_("meds", m.cat), sourceCat: m.cat, name: m.name, brand: m.brand != null ? String(m.brand).trim() : "", _custom: true, _delHideName: m.name }); } }); return entries; } function medMasterCats() { const s = uniqueDisplayCategories_("meds", medMasterEntries_()); if (!s.includes("その他")) s.push("その他"); return s; } function ensureMedItemsDelListener() { ["list-diseases", "list-meds"].forEach(id => { const el = document.getElementById(id); if (!el || el.dataset.delBound === "1") return; el.dataset.delBound = "1"; el.addEventListener("click", ev => { const rnm = ev.target.closest(".med-item-rename"); if (rnm) { ev.preventDefault(); ev.stopPropagation(); const typ = rnm.getAttribute("data-rn-type"); const cat = decodeURIComponent(rnm.getAttribute("data-rn-cat") || ""); if (typ === "meds") { const brand = decodeURIComponent(rnm.getAttribute("data-rn-brand") || ""); renameMasterMedicationRow_(cat, orig, brand, isCustom, cur); } else if (typ === "diseases") { renameMasterDiseaseRow_(cat, orig, isCustom, cur); const row = ev.target.closest(".med-item"); if (!row || !el.contains(row) || ev.target.closest(".med-item-del") || ev.target.closest(".med-item-rename")) return; ev.preventDefault(); const typ = row.getAttribute("data-med-type"); } function removeMasterItem(type, name, cat, isCustom) { if (!name || !cat) return; const dispCat = displayCatForType_(type, cat); if (!confirm(`マスタから「${name}」（${dispCat}）を削除しますか？\n※すでに選んでいる患者の選択はそのまま残ります。`)) return; } persistMasterPrefs_() .then(() => { renderMedItems(type); showToast("マスタから削除しました"); }) .catch(e => showToast("削除に失敗: " + (e && e.message ? e.message : String(e)))); } function sameMedMasterGridRow_(m, sourceCat, origName, origBrand, isCustom) { if (!!m._custom !== !!isCustom || m.sourceCat !== sourceCat) return false; String(m._origMedBrand).trim() : ""; const ob = origBrand != null ? e.message : String(e)))); } function addMasterCategory(type) { const label = type === "diseases" ? "全身疾患・既往歴" : "服薬情報"; const name = String(prompt(`${label}に追加するカテゴリー名を入力してください`, "") || "").trim(); if (!name) return; const cats = uniqueDisplayCategories_(type, type === "diseases" ? diseaseMasterEntries_() : medMasterEntries_()); if (cats.includes(name)) { showToast("同じカテゴリー名がすでにあります"); return; } if (type === "diseases") { customDiseaseCats.push(name); if (!diseaseCategoryOrder.includes(name)) { const o = diseaseCategoryOrder.length ? e.message : String(e)))); } function renameMasterCategory(type) { const entries = type === "diseases" ? diseaseMasterEntries_() : medMasterEntries_(); const cats = uniqueDisplayCategories_(type, entries); const current = medFilter[type] !== "all" ? medFilter[type] : (cats[0] || ""); const oldName = String(prompt("変更前のカテゴリー名を入力してください", current) || "").trim(); if (!oldName) return; if (!cats.includes(oldName)) { showToast("そのカテゴリーは見つかりません"); return; } const newName = String(prompt(`「${oldName}」の新しいカテゴリー名を入力してください`, oldName) || "").trim(); if (!newName || newName === oldName) return; if (cats.includes(newName)) { showToast("同じカテゴリー名がすでにあります"); return; } const renames = categoryRenamesForType_(type); const sourceCats = [...new Set(entries.filter(e => e.cat === oldName && !e._custom).map(e => e.sourceCat))]; sourceCats.forEach(src => { renames[src] = newName; }); if (type === "diseases") { customDiseases = normalizeCustomDiseasesEntries(customDiseases).map(e => e.cat === oldName ? medFilter[type] : (cats[0] || ""); const catName = String(prompt("削除するカテゴリー名を入力してください", current) || "").trim(); if (!catName) return; if (!cats.includes(catName)) { showToast("そのカテゴリーは見つかりません"); return; } if (!confirm(`カテゴリー「${catName}」をマスタ一覧から削除しますか？\n※すでに患者に選んでいる項目は残ります。`)) return; const targets = entries.filter(e => e.cat === catName); if (type === "diseases") { targets.forEach(e => { if (!hiddenDiseaseItems.some(h => h.cat === e.sourceCat && h.name === e.name)) hiddenDiseaseItems.push({ cat: e.sourceCat, name: e.name }); }); customDiseaseCats = normalizeMasterCategoryList_(customDiseaseCats.filter(c => c !== catName)); diseaseCategoryOrder = diseaseCategoryOrder.filter(c => c !== catName); } else { targets.forEach(e => { if (!hiddenMedItems.some(h => h.cat === e.sourceCat && h.name === e.name)) hiddenMedItems.push({ cat: e.sourceCat, name: e.name }); }); customMedCats = normalizeMasterCategoryList_(customMedCats.filter(c => c !== catName)); medCategoryOrder = medCategoryOrder.filter(c => c !== catName); } if (medFilter[type] === catName) medFilter[type] = "all"; persistMasterPrefs_() .then(() => { renderMedItems(type); showToast("カテゴリーを削除しました"); }) .catch(e => showToast("カテゴリー削除に失敗: " + (e && e.message ? e.message : String(e)))); } function restoreMasterItems(type) { const hidden = hiddenItemsForType_(type); if (!hidden.length) { showToast("復元できる削除済み項目はありません"); return; } const label = type === "diseases" ?     • `).join(""); } fill(ld, "diseases"); fill(lm, "meds"); } // ── アコーディオン開閉 ── function toggleAcc(id) { const body = document.getElementById(`acc-${id}`); const arrow = document.getElementById(`arrow-${id}`); const isOpen = body.classList.contains("open"); body.classList.toggle("open", !isOpen); arrow.classList.toggle("open", !isOpen); if (!isOpen) { if (id === "diseases") renderMedItems("diseases"); if (id === "meds") renderMedItems("meds"); } } // ── 医療情報の読み込み ── /** 旧UIの認知症記号（ローマ数字）→ 新フォーム（I, IIa…） */ const NINCHI_LEGACY_MAP = { "Ⅰ": "I", "Ⅱa": "IIa", "Ⅱb": "IIb", "Ⅲa": "IIIa", "Ⅲb": "IIIb", "Ⅳ": "IV" }; function loadMedicalInfo(pid) { customDiseases = []; customMeds = []; if (!pid || String(pid).trim() === "") { patientMedical = { conditions: [], medications: [], allergies: [], careLevel: "", independence: "", dementiaLevel: "", }; applyMedicalToUI(); document.getElementById("riskAlerts").innerHTML = ""; } else gasCall("getMedicalInfo", pid).then(json => { const data = JSON.parse(json); let dem = data.dementia_level || ""; if (dem && NINCHI_LEGACY_MAP[dem]) dem = NINCHI_LEGACY_MAP[dem]; patientMedical = { conditions: (data.conditions || []).map(normalizeMedEntry_).filter(x => x && x.name), medications: (data.medications || []).map(normalizeMedEntry_).filter(x => x && x.name), allergies: data.allergies || [], careLevel: data.care_level || "", independence:data.independence|| "", dementiaLevel: dem, }; if (applyExpandedMedicationsIfNeeded_() && selectedPatient) { saveMedicalInfo(); } applyMedicalToUI(); }).catch(e => { patientMedical = { conditions:[], medications:[], allergies:[], careLevel:"", independence:"", dementiaLevel:"" }; applyMedicalToUI(); showToast("医療情報の読み込みに失敗: " + (e && e.message ?     ` ).join(""); } // ── 初期化（openRecordから呼ぶ） ── function initMedicalInfo(pid) { patientMedical = { conditions:[], medications:[], allergies:[], careLevel:"", independence:"", dementiaLevel:"" }; medFilter = { diseases: "all", meds: "all" }; const ds = document.getElementById("search-diseases"); const ms = document.getElementById("search-meds"); if (ds) ds.value = ""; if (ms) ms.value = ""; buildCareLevelUI(); // アコーディオンを閉じる ["careLevel","diseases","meds","allergy"].forEach(id => { document.getElementById(`acc-${id}`)?.classList.remove("open"); document.getElementById(`arrow-${id}`)?.classList.remove("open"); }); document.getElementById("riskAlerts").innerHTML = ""; renderSelectedTags("diseases"); renderSelectedTags("meds"); renderAllergyTags(); updateCareLevelUI(); ["careLevel","diseases","meds","allergy"].forEach(id => updateAccBadge(id, 0)); loadMedicalInfo(pid); } // ── 治療履歴 ── function ensureHistoryListListener() { const el = document.getElementById("historyList"); if (!el || el.dataset.historyBound === "1") return; el.dataset.historyBound = "1"; el.addEventListener("click", onHistoryListClick); } function onHistoryListClick(e) { const openEl = e.target.closest("[data-history-open]"); if (openEl) { e.preventDefault(); const rid = openEl.getAttribute("data-history-open"); const rec = historyRecordsCache.find(x => String(x.id) === String(rid)); if (rec) openHistoryRecord(rec); return; } const delEl = e.target.closest("[data-history-delete]"); if (delEl) { e.preventDefault(); confirmDeleteHistoryRecord(delEl.getAttribute("data-history-delete")); } } function confirmDeleteHistoryRecord(recId) { if (!recId || !currentHistoryPatientId) return; if (!confirm("この診療記録を削除しますか？")) return; gasCall("deleteTreatmentRecord", recId).then(() => { localRecords = localRecords.filter(r => String(r.id) !== String(recId)); showToast("削除しました"); openHistory(currentHistoryPatientId); }).catch(e => showToast("削除に失敗: " + (e && e.message ?     `; return; } el.innerHTML = records.map((r, i) => { const fac = FACILITIES.find(f => f.id === r.fac_id); const isLatest = i === 0; const rid = r.id != null ?     ` : ""}
    `; }).join(""); } // ══════════════════════════════════════════ // 写真・X線 管理 // ══════════════════════════════════════════ let localPhotos = []; // { id, dataUrl, driveUrl, filename, category, dateTaken, patientId } let currentPhotoCat = "all"; let currentViewPhotoId = null; const PHOTO_CATS = ["口腔内","顔貌","義歯","X線","書類"]; /** 患者未登録の新規モーダルで追加した写真の仮 patientId（保存後に本 ID へ移す） */ const PHOTO_PENDING_NEW_ID = "__pending_new__"; /** Drive 写真を で出す用（PRIVATE + file.getUrl ではブラウザが読めないため file_id から埋め込みURLを組む） */ function patientPhotoDisplaySrc_(p) { if (!p) return ""; if (p.dataUrl) return p.dataUrl; const fid = p.id && !String(p.id).startsWith("tmp_") ? String(p.id) : ""; if (fid) return "https://drive.google.com/uc?export=view&id=" + encodeURIComponent(fid); const u = p.driveUrl ? String(photo.dataUrl).split(",")[1] : ""); if (!b64) { localPhotos = localPhotos.filter(p => p !== photo); return Promise.resolve(); } return gasCall("savePhoto", idStr, b64, photo.filename || "photo.jpg", photo.category || "口腔内", photo.dateTaken || "").then(result => { const r = JSON.parse(result); photo.id = r.fileId; photo.driveUrl = r.url; photo.patientId = idStr; delete photo.pendingBase64; delete photo.deferredUpload; }).catch(e => { showToast("写真の保存に失敗: " + (e && e.message ? e.message : String(e))); }); })); } // 患者の写真を読み込む function loadPhotos(patientId) { gasCall("getPhotos", patientId).then(json => { const photos = JSON.parse(json); photos.forEach(p => { const inline = p.inline_data_url ? } localPhotos.push({ id: p.file_id, dataUrl: inline || undefined, driveUrl: p.file_url, filename: p.filename, category: p.category, dateTaken: p.date_taken, patientId }); }); renderPhotoGrid(); }).catch(() => renderPhotoGrid()); } // ファイル選択 → プレビュー + カテゴリ選択 → アップロード function handlePhotoUpload(input) { const files = Array.from(input.files); if (!files.length) return; const pmId = document.getElementById("pm-id")?.value?.trim() || ""; const photoPid = (selectedPatient?.id && String(selectedPatient.id).trim()) || pmId; const draftInPatientModal = !photoPid && document.getElementById("patientModal")?.classList.contains("show"); if (!photoPid && !draftInPatientModal) { showToast("写真を追加する前に、患者を選ぶか「新しい患者を追加」で入力してください。"); const { dataUrl } = openPhotoCatModal._pending; const pmId = document.getElementById("pm-id")?.value?.trim() || ""; const pid = (selectedPatient?.id && String(selectedPatient.id).trim()) || pmId; const deferUpload = !pid && document.getElementById("patientModal")?.classList.contains("show"); renderPhotoGrid(); // GASに圧縮してアップロード（新規モーダルは患者保存後にまとめて送信） compressImage(dataUrl, 1000, 0.8, compressed => { const base64 = compressed.split(",")[1]; const photo = localPhotos.find(p => p.id === tempId); img.onload = () => { const canvas = document.createElement("canvas"); let w = img.width, h = img.height; if (w > maxPx || h > maxPx) { if (w > h) { h = Math.round(h * maxPx / w); w = maxPx; } else { w = Math.round(w * maxPx / h); [] : {}; cur = cur[key]; } const last = parts[parts.length - 1]; const lk = /^\d+$/.test(last) ? parseInt(last, 10) : last; cur[lk] = val; } function rptPullEdits_(container, root) { if (!container || !root) return; } function faxEmSpanClass_(kind) { if (kind === "red") return "fax-em-red"; if (kind === "hl") return "fax-em-hl"; if (kind === "box") return "fax-em-box"; return ""; } function faxEmMarkers_(kind) { const marks = { red: ["《赤》", "《/赤》"], hl: ["《黄》", "《/黄》"], box: ["【枠】", "【/枠】"] }; const RPT_DRAFT_CLOUD_CHUNK = 35000; function rptDraftStorageKey_(kind, id) { return `rptPreviewDraft_v${RPT_PREVIEW_DRAFT_VER}_${kind}_${String(id || "").replace(/[^\w\-_.]/g, "_")}`; } function rptReadLocalDraft_(kind, id) { if (!kind || !id) return null; return !!(res && res.ok); } const n = Math.ceil(envelope.length / RPT_DRAFT_CLOUD_CHUNK); for (let i = 0; i < n; i++) { await gasCall( "saveReportPreviewDraftChunk", kind, id, i, n, envelope.slice(i * RPT_DRAFT_CLOUD_CHUNK, (i + 1) * RPT_DRAFT_CLOUD_CHUNK) ); } const res = JSON.parse(await gasCall("saveReportPreviewDraftChunkFinish", kind, id)); return !!(res && res.ok); } catch (e) { return false; } } async function rptLoadDraftFromCloud_(kind, id) { try { const meta = JSON.parse(await gasCall("loadReportPreviewDraftInfo", kind, id)); } catch (e) {} } function rptSaveDraft_(kind, id, payload) { if (!kind || !id) return false; const savedAt = Date.now(); rptWriteLocalDraft_(kind, id, payload, savedAt); rptSaveDraftToCloud_(kind, id, payload, savedAt).catch(() => {});     `; return h; } let psPhotoDragState_ = null; function psFindPhoto_(patientIdx, photoId) { const ctx = lastPersonalSheetContext; const p = ctx && ctx.patients && ctx.patients[patientIdx]; if (!p || !p.photos) return null; const pid = String(photoId || ""); return p.photos.find(ph => String(ph.id || "") === pid) || null; } function psApplyPhotoWidgetStyle_(widget, ph) { if (!widget || !ph) return; widget.style.left = Math.round(Number(ph.x) || 0) + "px"; widget.style.top = Math.round(Number(ph.y) || 0) + "px"; widget.style.width = Math.max(48, Math.round(Number(ph.w) || 140)) + "px"; widget.style.transform = ""; const wrap = widget.querySelector(".ps-photo-img-wrap"); if (wrap) wrap.style.transform = "rotate(" + (Number(ph.rotate) || 0) + "deg)"; } function psClampPhotoInCanvas_(ph, widget, photosEl) { if (!photosEl || !ph) return; const cw = photosEl.clientWidth || 280; const ww = Math.max(48, parseFloat(widget && widget.style.width) || Number(ph.w) || 140); const wrap = widget && widget.querySelector(".ps-photo-img-wrap"); const rot = wrap ? psParseRotateDeg_(wrap.style.transform) : (Number(ph.rotate) || 0); const imgH = widget ? ph.y = Math.max(0, Math.round(ph.y || 0)); } function psUpdatePhotosContainerHeight_(photosEl) { if (!photosEl) return; let maxB = 72; photosEl.querySelectorAll(".ps-photo-widget").forEach(w => { const top = parseFloat(w.style.top) || 0; }); } }; container.addEventListener("click", onClick); container._psPhotoDownHandler = onDown; container._psPhotoClickHandler = onClick; } function buildPersonalSheetGridDocumentHtml_(ctx, forPrint) { const c = ctx || {};     `; h += renderPersonalSheetPatientPhotos_(p, i, forPrint); h += `
    `; } h += `
    `; return h; } function psPullPhotosFromRow_(row, patientObj) { const photos = []; row.querySelectorAll(".ps-photo-widget").forEach(w => { const img = w.querySelector("img"); const src = img && img.getAttribute("src"); if (!src) return; const wrap = w.querySelector(".ps-photo-img-wrap"); const rot = wrap ?     '; } function psRefreshPreview_(opts) { const skipPull = !!(opts && opts.skipPull); if (!skipPull) psPullPersonalSheetEdits_(); paintPersonalSheetPreview_(lastPersonalSheetContext); } function psRemovePatientAtIndex_(idx) { const ctx = lastPersonalSheetContext; if (!ctx || !ctx.patients) return; psPullPersonalSheetEdits_(); const i = parseInt(String(idx), 10); if (isNaN(i) || i < 0 || i >= ctx.patients.length) { showToast("除外対象が見つかりません"); return; } ctx.patients.splice(i, 1); ctx.patients = ctx.patients.filter(p => p && (p.patient_id || p.name || String(p.body || "").trim())); ctx.patient_count = ctx.patients.length; if (!ctx.patients.length) showToast("全員除外しました。再読み込みするか施設・年月を変えてください"); else showToast("患者を除外しました"); psRefreshPreview_({ skipPull: true }); } function psEnsureExtraComment_(idx) { const ctx = lastPersonalSheetContext; const p = ctx && ctx.patients && ctx.patients[idx]; if (!p) return; psPullPersonalSheetEdits_(); p._show_extra = true; if (!String(p.extra_comment || "").trim()) p.extra_comment = ""; psRefreshPreview_(); const host = document.getElementById("personalSheetPreviewInner"); const el = host && host.querySelector(`[data-rpt-path="patients.${idx}.extra_comment"]`); if (el) { try { el.focus(); } catch (_) {} } } function psPickPhotoForPatient_(idx, patientIdAttr) { psPullPersonalSheetEdits_(); const ctx = lastPersonalSheetContext; const pi = parseInt(String(idx), 10); let p = null; const pidAttr = patientIdAttr != null ?
